<div style="overflow:hidden;margin-bottom: 10px;    direction: ltr;">
<div class="is-containter" style="overflow:hidden;"><h3 style="font-size: 27px;">Unfortunately, Football World Rankings® are still on hold</h3><p>Due to lack of financial resources, we can no longer continue to publish the weekly rankings. Help us to keep the rankings alive. <b>A patron or sponsor,</b> who endorses our mission and makes the restart and further expansion possible, <b>is urgently needed.</b> Please contact the founder <a href="frank.verweijen@ifcstat.com" style="text-decoration-decoration:underline;"> frank.verweijen@ifcstat.com </a></p><p>It is certain that the Covid-19 pandemic has seriously affected the continuity and enjoyment of football. The established national leagues and international tournaments within continents are the enduring foundation on which football has become the greatest sport on the planet.</p><p>The Football World Rankings provide an additional measuring point. Clubs, coaches and top scorers from all continents feel recognized fairly while reflecting a fair weighting of the strength of each continent.</p><p><img class="showH" style="min-width:50px; max-width:150px; height:auto; float:left; margin-right:14px;display:none;" src="modules/images/Football_Frank.jpg"></p><p>This measurement function is increasingly appreciated. It is illustrated by the very strong increase in visitors and countless media worldwide referring to the rankings. It would be a big disappointment if the rankings disappear. Thank you in advance for all your efforts to keep us alive.</p><p><img class="hideH" style="min-width:50px; max-width:100px; height:auto; float:left; margin-right:14px" src="modules/images/Football_Frank.jpg">Kind regards, <br>Frank Verweijen<br>Founder of Football World Rankings.</p><p></p></div>
